## Text Elements

Accel-Sim is crucial today because it provides an extensively validated, extensible, near cycle-accurate open-source GPU simulator that lets researchers rapidly explore and model modern NVIDIA-like architectures and future design ideas without needing proprietary hardware details. ^beeFMOEn

Why Accel-Sim? ^jZKhe05G

Status… ^L7fNi2g6

Accel-Sim was originally developed as a collaboration between Purdue University, Northwestern University, and the University of British Columbia, and on GitHub it is actively maintained with recent commits, discussions, and a latest tagged release v1.3.0 in February 2025, indicating a current, production-ready and evolving framework. ^Q5ga2hPG

MemcpyHtoD,0x00007fa69d604000,65536

MemcpyHtoD,0x00007fa69d604000,65536 kernel-1-ctx_0x55656694dd90.trace.xz ^e9YB33gC

Compressed raw SASS inst. trace from NVBIT tracer tool ^24vvEQnN

Compressed post-processed "generic" trace reformatted into Accel-Sim's ISA-independent trace format ^NGPC6Ave

NVBit intercepts kernel launches (cuLaunchKernel), tracks contexts/cores/streams, and emits binary records with opcodes, registers, memory addresses (base+stride compressed), predicates, and metadata. Post-process with ./util/tracer_nvbit/post_process converts to .traceg ISA-independent format. ^iVAYTmvp

It allows to improvise, modify or find bottlenecks without having real access to the hardware. ^L5kGdNAf

Code testing before delopyment on real hardware ^8y8Q6Sz5

Using the run_simulation.py python script which launches accel-sim.out jobs per kernel locally. ^U0A9rZFr

or we can do it for specific Workloads : /gpu-simulator/bin/release/accel-sim.out -trace ./hw_run/rodinia_2.0-ft/9.1/backprop-rodinia-2.0-ft/4096___data_result_4096_txt/traces/kernelslist.g -config ./gpu-simulator/gpgpu-sim/configs/tested-cfgs/SM7_QV100/gpgpusim.config -config ./gpu-simulator/configs/tested-cfgs/SM7_QV100/trace.config ^WI6hWIUf

SASS Mode (RTX4090-SASS) : Trace-driven simulation from .traceg.xz files ^6KkvHsh9

PTX Mode (RTX4090-PTX) : Execution driven PTX emulation ^H6dJdUBX

-B <benchmark> ^YTkEgMa1

-C <config> ^8goxY9GR

-N <run_id> (name of the simulation) ^H3fBh174

-a <app_name> (for running specific apps from the benchmark) ^HNQ0wzeO

-T <trace_dir> (for defining the trace directory manually, i.e. a non-default trace location allocation) ^8J3Ng6UY

GPGPU-Sim is used as backend to the parced traces being generated by Accel-Sim frontend. ^E3fTetjp

The parsed traces is ISA-independent format. It uses gpgpusim.config and trace.config for cycle-accurate SM/Memory/interconnect simulation. ^FRGySY3N

The outputs from the simulation can be used for model validation, config tuning, or app/kernel perfomance stats generation. ^YWb9VKAX

using : ./util/job_launching/monitor_func_test.py -v -N <run_id> ^YozJGI0L

-v (VERBOSE) ^JmCjQKfL

-N <run_id> (NAME OF SIMULATION) ^rXqUJ69R

Runs NVIDIA profiler (nvprof/nsight-cli) on real GPU hardware to collect performance counters like cycles, IPC, cache stats, memory bandwidth for validation against simulation. ^tv1M4M6N

Takes benchmark suite (e.g., -B rodinia_2.0-ft) and optional profiler selection (--nsight_profiler --disable_nvprof). ^UQwzTAHS

Hardware counter CSVs in ./hw_run/<device>/<cuda_version>/ containing per-kernel performance metrics (cycles, IPC, L1/L2 hits, bandwidth, occupancy). ^QeoUAiUy

Stats Collection ^V7rKxqHG

How's it done? ^CKsNyrik

./util/job_launching/get_stats.py -N <run_id> | tee stats.csv aggregates stats.txt from all sims into normalized CSV with kernel/config metrics ^2kku8Oqd

Store format: ^1tLjuLUC

Parameters ^cU6eKVnz

-R (per-kernel), -k (kernel stats), -K (kernel-level), -B <benchmark>, -C <config>, -N <run_id> ^ZVd1Atmy

Requirements ^nAzFB3r4

Necessity? ^F9yQWYXY

Requires physical NVIDIA GPU access; same compute capability as simulated target (e.g., V100 for QV100 configs); nvprof/nsight-cli installed; apps pre-built ^CH0kqnbc

Validates simulator accuracy by counter-by-counter comparison; identifies bugs/misrepresentations in memory coalescing, cache sectoring, L1 adaptive behavior ^DfSjHupF

0 : Follow accel-sim manual for complete descriptions. ^g79ZyCgC

1. Create hw_def.h header with minimal hardware specs (SM count, warp size, L1/L2 sizes), compile microbenchmarks (l1_lat, l1_bw, l2_bw, mem_bw) ^gCsqFHNP

2 : run ./util/tuner/GPU_Microbenchmark/run_all.sh | tee stats.txt ^uP6Z0A91

3 : execute ./util/tuner/tuner.py -s stats.txt to auto-generate config files. ^aqj01XOr

Automatically discovers undocumented architectural parameters (L1/L2 sectoring, adaptive cache policies, memory coalescing rules, sub-warp behaviors) by fitting microbenchmark results to GPGPU-Sim models. ^FMHaxZCh

Expect 5-20% cycle error after initial tuning; memory system tuning (L1 latency, L2 bandwidth, DRAM timing) yields largest accuracy gains. ^70byCz0Y

Tuner cannot model architectural changes across GPU generations (e.g., Volta→Turing tensor cores); manual correlation analysis required for major discrepancies; tuning only optimizes GPGPU-Sim params, not ISA simulation correctness. ^LOv8mTpd

WELCOME!! ^4XxvIMjn

- Basically copy the entire 3070 configs directory in ./gpu-simulator/gpgpu-sim/configs/tested-cfgs/ & ./gpu-simulator/configs/tested-cfgs/ and rename it to your desired 4090 config folder name.
- Add it to define-standard-cfgs.yml. Generate the 4090 config using tuner section in accel-sim.
- Copy the config parameters from the newly generated one to the renamed copy_of_3070 config.
- Add the ISA support for 4090 by using the ISA file of RTX3070 from ISA_Def folder.
- Add the above support in ./gpu-simulator/trace-driven/trace_driven.cc
- Add RTX4090 to config_maps = {} in ./util/plotting/correl_mappings.py.  
and include the 4090 ISA created in STEP 1 above to ./gpu-simulator/trace-driven/trace_driven.cc

- Also do copy the trace.config from 3070 directory, in tested-cfgs folder to the 4090 config folder in same. ^QSJCNkAW
